              <h3><a href="/blogs/magazine/from-unrecorded-to-recorded-deadstock-gets-a-new-lease-on-life">From Unrecorded to Recorded: Deadstock gets a new lease on life.</a></h3>

              
                <div class="meta meta--after-title small-text">
                  <div class="iconmeta time">
                    
                      <time datetime="2021-03-05T12:23:31Z">March 5, 2021</time>
                    
                    
                      —
                      <span class="author">Clean Canvas</span>
                    
                  </div>
                </div>
              
<div class="rte"><meta charset="utf-8"><span>Spawning from our principled outlook, we launched the Recorded collection. The aim to create awareness of today’s mass consumption and how disposable goods are inextricably linked to this phenomenon.</span>

              <h3><a href="/blogs/magazine/true-sustainability-is-quality-that-lasts-a-lifetime">True sustainability is quality that lasts a lifetime.</a></h3>

              
                <div class="meta meta--after-title small-text">
                  <div class="iconmeta time">
                    
                      <time datetime="2021-03-05T12:22:15Z">March 5, 2021</time>
                    
                    
                      —
                      <span class="author">Clean Canvas</span>
                    
                  </div>
                </div>
              
<div class="rte"><meta charset="utf-8"><span>When it comes to thinking sustainably across the whole business, we believe that few come close to Unrecorded. More than a mere label, we think that sustainability is a doing word. To be sustainable is to last more than a lifetime. For us, strong apparel should be at the heart of any sustainable fashion project.</span>
</div><div class="article__read-more-container">
